## Morghul
*Eternal Avatar of Corruption*<br>
**Habitat:** Any except Underwater & Urban; **Treasure:** Any <br>
When the Sun goeth down and hideth its face beneath the edge of the world, and only the small stars remain to watch the turning Earth, and the little fires of men flicker in scattered towns and villages—then is the hour when the Watch is kept. Soldiers and Guards stand upon the old walls and in the old towers, their eyes turned to the dark places, watching for that which moveth under cover of night and cometh not with invitation, bringing sorrow and fear in its wake.
And as they watch, they speak low among themselves, telling dark tales not to comfort, but to sharpen the soul with fear, that weariness may not close the eye, nor dreams lull the vigilant.

They speak of a creature that rose alone from the blackened marshes, and wandered the wide Earth, coming at last to the gates of the cities of men. There it stood and called for kings, wishing only to bestow its gifts. What those gifts were, none now dare say—but those kings who took them wailed horribly and fled into the wilderness, as their cities toppled and burned.
They speak also of the thing that climbeth the mountain slopes in the hours when the Moon hideth her face. It is not alone, for behind it go the malformed—things of twisted limb and broken shape, who cry out for others yet dwelling upon the mountain, those who found no refuge in the ancient halls carved into stone. And the malformed call to them, saying: Come, be as we are. Join the parade of hatred and of grief.

\columnbreak

<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>

They speak, too, of a village that was swallowed by a malicious wood. If one enter into the heart of that place, they shall find rusted gates, and buildings distorted and bent. And at their base crawl men and women upon all fours, hoofed and clawed, snarling like beasts. And within the shattered homes walk creatures upon two legs, clad in the tatters of human garb, speaking in tongues unknown—barking and hissing in a language that may not be broken.

In the center of that accursèd place groweth a tree, and it thrashèth and writhes like a beast snared in iron. Beneath its roots lieth a cave, and the walls thereof are of glass that floweth like the sea in storm. And within—He who is master of torment and of chaos. His desires are caught in the glass and move upon its surface, unspoken and undying.
Yet the Watchers know not that all these things, and more besides, are but the workings of one and the same. A spirit vile, who went forth upon the land ere the world was given its names. Since that time it hath crept and stalked and slithered in manifold forms, each more loathsome than the last. Wherever it goeth, there spring up mutability and madness, and chaos bloometh in its wake.
Other terrible beasts seek out the Thing of Old, that they might be given bodies of dreadful might. Their forms are shaped by the churning Chaos that eternally followeth the One who hath worn so many guises.

It seeketh not dominion, nor worship. It seeketh only that Order shall be unmade and forgotten.


<img src='https://i.postimg.cc/kX9b47kJ/Boneyard-Lurker-5000x.jpg' style='position:absolute; top:-80px; right:-220px; width:1200px;' />

  style='position:absolute;right:-144px;top:135px;height:1400px;width:1416px;transform:rotate(192deg)' />

\pagebreakNum

### Morghul's Lair
Wherever Morghul makes his lair, the world around him twists like clay in the hands of a mad sculptor. Stone flows like water, reshaping itself into horrid architecture; trees contort into impossible forms as their bark peels away to reveal skin beneath. All manner of misbegotten creatures circle his domain—drawn to this locus of chaos, hoping to be reborn in the presence of the Lord of Mutations.


When fighting within his lair, the Morghul's Challenge Rating (CR) increases by 1.  

#### Lair Actions  

On initiative count 1 (losing initiative ties), the lair chooses two unoccupied spaces at the edge of its boundaries. A Wicked Beast (stat block on the page after next) appears in each space and remains until destroyed. They act on initiative count 0 (losing initiative ties).

#### Regional Effects  

The presence of Morghul has a drastic impact on his surroundings, spreading corruption within a 10-mile radius of his lair that causes the following effects:

* Any creature in the area that ends its turn with three or more mutations gains a random deformity from the Deformities Table below. A creature cannot gain another deformity this way for 1 minute.

* Any creature that finishes a long rest within the area must succeed on a DC 20 Charisma saving throw or gain a random deformity from the Deformities Table below.

These deformities persist until the *greater restoration* or *heal* spell is cast on the affected creature. However, you may choose to make the removal of deformities more difficult—turning them into a long-term plot hook or quest. Below are example methods for removing them:

##### Removing Deformaties

| 1d4 |  Example     |
|:---:|:-----------|
|  1  | **The Sculptor Witch.** Tales speak of a strange witch who is both young and old. She works with white clay that she shapes into perfect likenesses of those who visit her. Any who gaze upon their statue may transfer a deformity into the sculpture—forever trapped in hardened clay. |
|  2  | **The Spring of Silence.** Deep within a gloom-stricken forest overrun by the restless dead lies a sacred spring. Its waters remain untouched by decay, an oasis that the cursed creatures of the wood dare not enter. Any who are baptized in its pure, silver waters are cleansed of their deformities. |
|  3  | **The Feast Below.** In the ruins of an abandoned village lies a cellar leading to vast catacombs, warmly lit and filled with unspoiled wine and impossible feasts. Gold lines the walls, and silken drapes hang. Here dwell radiant and alruing demons (Mariliths) who offer to remove any deformity with a single touch. But they will not stop at peeling away your deformities.

|  |       |
|:---:|:-----------|
|  4  | **The Moonbound Procession.** A procession of deformed spirits walks the world in mourning, visible only by the full moon’s light. Those who can predict their path and walk beside them from dusk to dawn will find a new spirit joins their ranks by morning with thier deformations transfer upon it.

<Br>

##### Deformities Table

|1d20 |        |
|:---:|:-----------|
|  1  | One massive, goat-like eye sits in the center of your forehead. |
|  2  | A mane of thick, oily hair grows down your spine that stands on end when you are angry. |
|  3  | Malformed, asymmetrical horns jut from your skull at odd angles. |
|  4  | Your face resembles a twisted beast’s muzzle. |
|  5  | Your legs bend like a goat’s, ending in cracked, blackened hooves. |
|  6  | Your skin is thick, leathery, and covered in patches of dark scales. |
|  7  | A second mouth sits sideways across your throat. It opens when you're angry or excited. |
|  8  | Your fingers are overly long, with too many joints, ending in sharp nails. |
|  9  |  A useless third arm hangs limp and spasming every now and then. |
| 10  | Your mouth is filled with rows of mismatched teeth that slowly fall out and regrow over time. |
| 11  | Your facial skin sheds daily like a snake’s molting. |
| 12  | Thin spines grow along your limbs, twitching when touched. |
| 13  | Small, insectile wings sprout from your back, flapping ineffectively. |
| 13  | Two tails drag behind you—one forked, the other bristled like a bottlebrush.. |
| 14  | Your tongue is thick, forked, and moves independently, tasting the air like a serpent. |
| 15  | One side of your body is covered in feathers that shift colors rapidly. |
| 16  | Tiny branches with Small blood-red leaves cover your body. |
| 17  | Twitching antennae grow from your skull. |
| 18  | You sweat rainbow ichor, staining clothes and leaving a sickly sweet scent. . |
| 19  | Your flesh become trasnluents allowing your orgains and bones to be seen. |
| 20  | Strange runes are carved into your flesh, writhing and shifting across your body. |

>
> ### Traits
>
> ***Adaptive Morphing.*** When Morghul fails a saving throw that required his action to make or when he fails a saving throw at the beginning or end of a turn, he can choose to succeed instead and takes force damage equal to 2d10 + the amount by which he failed the save.
>
> ***Aura of Transmutation.*** Morghul emits an aura in a 30‑foot emanation from himself. Any ranged attack that travels 15 feet or more through the emanation automatically misses. Spells and other magical effects can't extend into or out of the emanation. Each creature that ends its turn in the aura must make a *Charisma saving throw:* DC 15. <br> *Failure:* The creature suffers a random mutation from the Mutation Table on the page after next (*Mutation Save DC 15*). On a failure of 5 or more, it gains two mutations; by 10 or more, it gains three mutations.
>
> ***Demonic Restoration.*** If Morghul dies, he returns to life in 4d4 × 10 years and regains all his hit points.
>
> ### Actions
>
> ***Writhing Attack.*** Morghul performs two of the following actions at random. He can take these actions at any point during his turn, in any order:
> - **1. Shredding Claw.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 18 (4d8) slashing damage. If this attack scores a critical hit, it deals an extra 10 (3d6) slashing damage.
> - **2. Erupting Flames.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, reach 15 ft., one target. *Hit:* 18 (4d8) fire damage. If the target is a creature or flammable object, it ignites. Until a creature takes an action to douse the fire, the target takes 10 (3d6) fire damage at the end of each of its turns.
> - **3. Morbid Strike.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 18 (4d8) necrotic damage, and the target can’t regain hit points until the start of Morghul’s next turn.
> - **4. Shadow Spear.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, reach 30 ft., one target. *Hit:* 18 (4d8) cold damage, and the target can’t see more than 5 feet until the start of Morghul’s next turn.
> - **5. Slimy Tendril.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, reach 30 ft., one target. *Hit:* 18 (4d8) poison damage, and the target is pulled 30 feet toward Morghul.
> - **6. Destabilizing Touch.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 18 (4d8) force damage, and the target has disadvantage on its next saving throw against Morghul’s Aura of Transmutation.
>
> ### Essence of Chaos
>
> When Morghul rolls initiative, he calls upon the Dark Powers to warp the world around him. For 1 minute—or until Morghul dies—the Dark Powers (Intelligence 16) act in his best interest. On initiative count 20 (losing ties),  one of the following effects is selected at random, and the powers then choose a point within 60 feet of Morghul; the effect occurs in a 15‑foot cube centered on that point:
>
> - **1. Booming Roar.** *Constitution saving throw:* DC 18, each creature in the area. <br> *Failure:* The creature takes 18 (4d8) thunder damage and is sheathed in booming energy until initiative count 20 on the next round. If it willingly moves 5 feet or more before then, it takes 13 (3d8) thunder damage and the effect ends. <br>*Success:* Half damage.
> - **2. Snaring Vines.** *Dexterity or Strength saving throw (target’s choice): DC 18,* each creature in the area. <br> *Failure:* The creature takes 18 (4d8) bludgeoning damage and is restrained by vines until they are destroyed (AC 15; 30 HP; vulnerable to slashing). <Br> *Success:* Half damage.
> - **3. Distorted Space.** *Charisma saving throw: DC 18,* each creature in the area. <br> *Failure:* The creature takes 18 (4d8) force damage and is teleported to an unoccupied space of the Dark Powers’ choice within the cube that it can see. The chosen space must support the creature without squeezing.
> - **4. Spreading Nightmares.** *Wisdom saving throw: DC 18,* each creature in the area. <br> *Failure:* The creature takes 18 (4d8) psychic damage and becomes frightened until initiative count 20 of the next round. <br> *Success:* Half damage. When the fear ends (even early), each other creature within 10 feet of the affected creature (excluding Morghul) takes 18 (4d8) psychic damage.

> ***Rend.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 10 (2d6 + 3) slashing damage.

### Epic Battle: Unbound Abomination
If you wish to make Morghul into a true threat worthy of providing the final battle to a campaign, you can double his maximum hit points, bringing the total up to 594 hit points, and give him the Unbound Abomination ability. This increases his CR to 21.

***Unbound Abomination (Recharges after a Short or Long Rest).***  If Morghul is reduced to half his hit points (297 or less), he may end any effects incapacitating, and he chooses two unoccupied spaces within 15 feet, causing a thing of chaos (stat block on the previous page,) to appear in each space. They act on their own turns On initiative count 0 (losing initiative ties). 

Additionally, for the next hour, Morghul's size becomes Large, and when he uses his Writhing Attack action, he can now perform three attacks instead of two.

### Mutations
Whenever an effect calls for mutating a creature, choose one of the effects from the table below at random.
##### Mutation Table
| d6  | Mutation |  Creature Effect  |
|:---:|:---------:| :---------:|
|  1  |  Wild Spasms | The creature can't take reactions, and on each of its turns it must choose whether it gets a move, an action, or a bonus action; it gets only one of the three. |
|  2  | Degeneration  | The creature's form becomes brittle.  While a creature is brittle, any attack that hits the creature is a critical hit.|
|  3  | Twisted Arms |  The creature can no longer wield weapons or cast spells with somatic components and it has disadvantage on all weapon attack rolls.|
|  4  | Inverted Eyes | The creature is blinded.|
|  5  | Gelatinous Legs | The creature falls prone and can't stand up.|
|  6  | Regeneration | The creature regains 10 hit points at the start of its turn if it has at least 1 hit point.|



\columnbreak

### Sealing the Spirit of Chaos

Morghul is an eternal spirit of chaos—death is merely a delay to his return. However, if you wish to give your players a way to end Morghul’s cycle of rebirth once and for all, consider using one of the following methods:

| Method  | Description | Outcome
|:---:|:-----------:|:-----------:|
|  The Tome of Final Binding  | A blank tome with ever-hungry pages can trap Morghul if a prophet of great power records his wicked deeds within.       |  Morghul is sealed inside the tome. If the book is destroyed or read aloud, he is released.   |
|  The Grove of Reckoning  | If defeated in a sacred grove blessed by archfey, Morghul’s power can be drained and consumed by these ancient beings.       | Morghul is prevented from returning. However, the consequences of the archfey absorbing his chaotic essence are unknown.      | 
|  The Mirror of Dread Reflection  | A legendary mirror reacts to Morghul’s reflection, becoming a portal to a nightmare realm shaped by his hatred.       | If Morghul is forced through the mirror and it is shattered, he is trapped in a prison of his own making.      |
|  The Shattered Name  | Morghul’s true name was shattered and scattered across the world, embedded in beasts, trees, and relics.      | If all fragments are gathered and his true name restored, Morghul assumes a final, nightmarish form—one that can be permanently destroyed.      | 

 <img src='https://i.postimg.cc/y8TmyDCr/Grimoire-of-the-Dead.jpg' style='position:absolute;right:-0px;bottom:-220px;width:816px;transform:scaleX(-1)' />

<img src='https://www.gmbinder.com/images/cPPYV7h.png' 
style='position:absolute;right:-280px;top:-320px;height:1400px;width:1416px;transform:rotate(-5deg)' />

### Morghul's Tactics
Morghul's attacks are determined randomly, but he applies a strategy based on the mutations of his targets. Each attack favors specific conditions or mutations.

#### Writhing Attacks
* **Shredding Claw.** Targets a creature with the Degeneration mutation.
* **Erupting Flames.** Targets a creature with the Wild Spasms mutation, or those not adjacent to any allies.
* **Morbid Strike.** Targets creatures with the Regeneration mutation.
* **Shadow Spear.** Targets ranged creatures.
* **Slimy Tendrils.** Targets ranged creatures or those with the Gelatinous Legs or Inverted Eyes mutations.
* **Destabilizing Touch.** Targets creatures with low Charisma, or those with Gelatinous Legs or Inverted Eyes.

#### Essence of Chaos
This ability always targets the largest group of creatures. If multiple groups have the same number of targets, the Dark Powers choose based on which mutations they can exploit:

* **Booming Roar.** Targets the group with the fewest mutations.
* **Snaring Vines.** Targets creatures with Twisted Arms and Wild Spasms.
* **Distorted Space.** Targets creatures with Gelatinous Legs.
* **Spreading Nightmares.** Also targets creatures with Gelatinous Legs.

#### Lair Effects
* Wicked Beasts created by the lair attack creatures they have advantage against.
* Once a Wicked Beast transforms into a Thing of Chaos, it uses the same targeting logic as Morghul to determine its attacks.

### Morghul's Loot
Valuable loot dropped by Morghul typically comes from harvested materials found amongst his deformed remains and usually requires a **Wisdom (Survival)** or **Intelligence (Arcana)** check. You may also allow players proficient in specific tools to harvest relevant items (e.g., a **Wisdom (Leatherworker’s Tools)** check to gather Hide). 

##### Morghul Loot (Avg. 1,800gp)

| Looting Check Result <br> or 1d20 + 7 |  Loot  |
|:---:|:-----------:|
|  1-9  | 1 500gp Items (500gp) |
|  10-14 | 1 1,000gp Item (1,000gp) | 
|  15-21 | 1d4(2) 1,000gp Items (2,000gp) |  
|  22-25 | 1 2,000gp Items (2,000gp)  |  
|  26+ |  1d4(2) 2,000gp Items (4,000gp) |  

\columnbreak

#### Optional: Describing Looted Materials
If you’re not interested in the specifics, simply say the party collected materials worth the rolled gp value. If you want more detail, the tables below suggest materials for different gp values by creature. They also provide **Example Names** and **Quality Descriptors** for items worth **half** or **twice** the table's gp value.

For example, a 1,000gp Bone item from Morghul could be Morghul's Horn, a 500gp version might be a Morghul's Cracked Horn, and a 2,000gp version could be a Morghul's Prime Horn.

***When To Use Descriptions.*** You can describe these items during looting, when selling them, or when crafting, but it's best not to make players track long descriptive names. Only use as much detail as is needed when needed.



##### Morghul Materials: 1,000gp 

|1d6 | Material | Example Name (Quality Descriptors) | 
|:--:|:---:|:-----------:|
| 1   | Bone|  Morghul's Horn (Cracked/Prime) | 
| 2   | Cloth | Morghul's Cowl (Tattered/Prime)|  
| 3   | Hide | Morghul's Hide (Tattered/Prime)|  
| 4   | Flesh |  Morghul's Flesh (Stringy/Prime) |  
| 5  | Fluid |Morghul's Blood (Diluted/Prime) | 
| 6  | Wood |Morghul's Totem Scraps (Damaged/Prime) | 

#### Optional: Magic Loot for Item Crafting

If you plan to use harvested loot for crafting magic items, you can try to thematically align the effects of the magic items being crafted with the creature's they're harvested from. In Morghul's case, Chaos effects would make the most sense. These would be magic item effects that warp reality or induce mutations or madness in their targets.

***Magic Loot GP Values.*** The value of magic ingredients depends on your crafting system. Subtract their cost from the normal loot’s gp value. If the ingredient is worth significantly more, subtract it from the next treasure hoard instead.

## Spawns of Chaos
*Mutant Abominations Warped By The Power of Chaos*<br>
**Habitat:** Any; **Treasure:** None <br>
Over untold ages, as chaotic realms have breached  <br> mortal plane, these incursions have birthed a plethora of abominations, their malign influence twisting all caught in their path. Some creatures, bathed in mutating energies, become beings that defy all logic and order. These nightmarish anomalies are broadly known as spawns of chaos.

These cosmic mockeries arise in myriad ways—perhaps a warrior of the Dark Gods is bestowed with too many "blessings" from their fickle patron, warping their body beyond recognition. Or a sorcerer foolishly channels raw power from the distant realms, their body and mind fracturing under the strain of such immense magic. Others undergo this cruel metamorphosis merely by standing in the presence of a virulent monument or a great herald of the Ruinous Gods.

Though the means of a spawn’s creation are countless, their forms and abilities are infinite. Some are grotesque amalgamations of limbs from men and beasts, fused into a disorienting and horrifying jumble. Others bear the heads of massive insects, cloaked in coarse, woolly hair, crowned with stag-like antlers or sharp beaks that part to reveal rows of human teeth. Some possess powerful equine limbs that end in fleshy, flowering patterns of fingers, each tipped with a wicked stinger.

\columnbreak

<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>

Others are even more bizarre—composed almost entirely of raw, corded muscle, riddled with jagged bony protrusions and snapping jaws strewn haphazardly across their hulking figures. Some are little more than writhing masses of snake-like tendrils, their soft, silken skin crisscrossing as they release strange, intoxicating scents and sounds that enrapture those unfortunate enough to encounter them.

More grotesque still are those whose bloated forms are covered in shifting tumors and sores, rupturing under their own strain to release all manner of putrid mucus. Most bizarre of all, however, are those whose unstable forms are not composed of any organic material—lumps of flowing metal or wax, their ever-shifting surfaces revealing fleeting visages that scream, letting loose gouts of colorful flames and light before melting back into the mass.

Whatever monstrous configuration these epitomes of discord take, they all share an inherent instability in their existence. All spawns of chaos are erratic and violent, destroying anything their impulsive whims lead them to. Ultimately, all are doomed—either to die in conflict or to be torn apart by the very energies that birthed them.

<img src='https://i.postimg.cc/MTZYxy2t/Delraich-Mercadian-Masques-Mt-G-Art.jpg' style='position:absolute; top:-35px; right:-10px; width:848px;' />

<img src='https://www.gmbinder.com/images/WGybwnz.png' style='position:absolute; top:216px; right:90px; width:950px; filter:  grayscale(00%) brightness(97%); transform:rotate(20deg)' />

<img src='https://www.gmbinder.com/images/WGybwnz.png' style='position:absolute; top:310px; right:-30px; width:900px; filter:  grayscale(00%) brightness(97%); transform:rotate(0deg)' />


\pagebreakNum

##### Spawn of Chaos Adventure Hooks

| 1d6  | Plot Hook |
|:---:|:-----------:|
|  1  | **The Mutating Ruins:** An ancient ruin, long sealed away, has begun to leak strange, reality-warping energy. Locals whisper of travelers who entered and emerged twisted beyond recognition, or worse, never returned at all. The players are sent to investigate and navigate a crumbling labyrinth where the walls pulse with unnatural life and spawns of chaos formed from the fused bodies of previous explorers lurk.  |
|  2  | **The Cursed Champion:** A mighty warrior devoted to the Dark Gods has been "blessed" too many times, their body grotesquely twisted into a monstrous Spawn of Chaos. However, their former warband refuses to let them die, instead worshiping them as a divine avatar. The players must infiltrate this zealous warband, fight through hordes of fanatics, and put down the rampaging spawn before its mutations spread further. |
|  3  | **The Flesh Hive:** A once-thriving town has become eerily silent, its streets overgrown with strange, pulsating growths. Those who enter are greeted by whispers in the walls, disjointed limbs sprouting from cobblestone, and flesh melding into wood and iron. The town’s people have been consumed, fused together into a colossal Spawn of Chaos, which now writhes beneath the town square, birthing lesser horrors that crawl through the ruins. |


\columnbreak

<br><br><br>

|  | |
|:---:|:-----------:|
|  4  | **The Eldritch Caravan:** A traveling merchant caravan arrives in town, selling rare and exotic wares. However, strange occurrences begin—shadows stretch in the wrong direction, people wake up changed, and some disappear entirely. The caravan’s leader has unknowingly acquired a relic that is birthing Spawns of Chaos in the night, twisting both people and objects into abominations. The players must investigate before the town is lost to corruption. |
|  5  | **The Tower of Madness:** An abandoned wizard’s tower has become a beacon of chaos, warping the landscape around it. Inside, space folds in on itself, corridors loop endlessly, and doors lead to nowhere. The wizard, long since consumed by their own experiments, has transformed into a monstrous Spawn of Chaos, their body fusing with their spellbooks and laboratory equipment, turning the tower into a living nightmare.  |
|  6  | **The Living Battlefield:** A war long ago was fought on cursed ground, and now, the battlefield itself refuses to rest. The bodies of the dead have merged into a horrific Spawn of Chaos, a lumbering mass of bone, armor, and flesh that shifts unpredictably. The players must destroy it before it awakens fully, lest it rampage across the land, absorbing everything in its path. |

> ### Traits
> ***Immutable Form.*** The spawn is immune to any spell or effect that would alter its form.  
>
> ***Shambling Horror.*** At the start of the spawn's turn, its walking speed increases by 1d6 × 10 feet until the start of its next turn.  
>
> ### Actions
> ***Writhing Attack.*** The spawn performs two of the following actions at random. It can take these actions at any point during its turn, in any order:  
> - **1. Claws.** The spawn makes two attacks. *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 10 (3d6) slashing damage.  
> - **2. Tentacle.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 15 ft., *Hit:* 17 (5d6) bludgeoning damage, and the target is pulled 15 feet toward the spawn.  
> - **3. Bite.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 17 (5d6) piercing damage. If the target is Medium or smaller, it must make a *Dexterity Saving Throw:* DC 13. *Failure:* It becomes grappled (escape DC 13) and is restrained.  
> - **4. Ram.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 14 (4d6) bludgeoning damage. If the spawn moved 20 or more feet straight toward the target immediately before hitting, the target takes an extra 7 (2d6) piercing damage and must make a *Strength Saving Throw:* DC 13. *Failure:* It is knocked prone.  
> - **5. Flail.** The spawn makes an attack against any number of creatures within 5 feet of it. *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 10 (3d6) bludgeoning damage.  
>- **6. Bash.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 17 (5d6) bludgeoning damage, and the target must make a *Constitution Saving Throw:* DC 13. *Failure:* It is dazed* until the end of the spawn's next turn.

### Lesser Spawn of Chaos Alternative Writhing Attack Tables

The following are additional action sets for the spawn's Writhing Attack, which can be used instead of its normal set. Each set is organized thematically, but feel free to mix and match to create your own table of six.


##### Lesser Spawn of Rage Table  
| 1d6  | Actions | Effect |
|:---:|:-----------|:-----------|
| 1 | **Mangling Talons** | *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 14 (4d6) slashing damage, and the target must make a *Strength Saving Throw:* DC 13. *Failure:* The target suffers a rending wound. While wounded, the target has disadvantage on Strength, Dexterity, and Constitution d20 Tests, and its speed is halved. The wound ends if the creature regains 15 or more hit points at once, or if the target or a creature within 5 feet of it uses an action to stanch the wound by succeeding on a Wisdom (Medicine) check: DC 13.|
| 2 | **Bone Spike** | *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 10 (3d6) piercing damage. If the spawn moved at least 20 feet straight toward the target immediately before this hit and the target is Large or smaller, it is impaled on the spike and becomes grappled (escape DC 13). While grappled, the target is restrained and takes 3 (1d6) piercing damage at the start of each of the spawn’s turns. |
| 3 | **War Stomp** | *Dexterity or Strength Saving Throw (target’s choice):* DC 13, each other creature in a 10-foot emanation from the spawn. If the ground in that area is loose earth or stone, it becomes difficult terrain until cleared. *Failure:* The creature takes 7 (2d6) bludgeoning damage and is knocked prone. |
| 4 | **Flesh Feast** | *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 10 (3d6) piercing damage, and the spawn regains hit points equal to the damage dealt. |
| 5 | **Blood Disgorge** | *Constitution Saving Throw:* DC 13 each creature in a 30-foot cone. *Failure:* The creature takes 10 (3d6) necrotic damage and can’t regain hit points until the start of the spawn’s next turn. *Success:* Half damage only |
| 6 | **Murderous Fit** | The spawn’s speed increases by 20 feet until the end of its turn, and it can make up to three attacks. Each attack must be against a different target. *Melee Weapon Attack:* +5 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 10 (3d6) bludgeoning damage. |

> - **Challenge** 7 (2,900 XP); **Proficiency Bonus** +3
> ___
> ### Traits
> ***Immutable Form.*** The spawn is immune to any spell or effect that would alter its form.  
>
> ***Shambling Horror.*** At the start of the spawn's turn, its walking speed increases by 1d6 × 10 feet until the start of its next turn.
>
> ### Actions
> ***Writhing Attack.*** The spawn performs two of the following actions at random. It can take these actions at any point during its turn, in any order:  
> - **1. Claws.** The spawn makes two attacks. *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 16 (3d10) slashing damage.  
> - **2. Tentacle.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 15 ft., *Hit:* 27 (5d10) bludgeoning damage, and the target is pulled 15 feet toward the spawn.  
> - **3. Bite.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 22 (4d10) piercing damage. If the target is a Medium or smaller creature, it must make a *Dexterity Saving Throw:* DC 15. *Failure:* The target is swallowed by the spawn (up to four creatures can be swallowed at a time).  While swallowed, the target is blinded and restrained, has total cover against attacks and effects outside the spawn, and takes 11 (2d10) acid damage at the start of each of the spawn's turns. 
> If the spawn takes 20 or more damage on a single turn from a creature inside it, the spawn must succeed on a Constitution saving throw (DC 15) at the end of that turn or regurgitate all swallowed creatures, which fall prone within 10 feet of it. If the spawn dies, any swallowed creature is no longer restrained and can escape from the corpse by using 20 feet of movement, exiting prone.  
> - **4. Ram.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 22 (4d10) bludgeoning damage. If the spawn moved 20 or more feet straight toward the target immediately before hitting, the target takes an extra 11 (2d10) piercing damage and must make a *Strength Saving Throw:* DC 15. *Failure:* It is knocked prone.  
> - **5. Flail.** The spawn makes an attack against any number of creatures within 5 feet of it. *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 16 (3d10) bludgeoning damage.  
> - **6. Bash.** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 27 (5d10) bludgeoning damage, and the target must make a *Constitution Saving Throw: DC 15.* *Failure:* It is dazed* until the end of the spawn's next turn.
>

### Spawn of Chaos Alternative Writhing Attack Tables

The following are additional action sets for the spawn's Writhing Attack, which can be used instead of its normal set. Each set is organized thematically, but feel free to mix and match to create your own table of six.


##### Chaos Spawn of Rage Table
| 1d6  | Actions | Effect |
|:---:|:-----------|:-----------|
| 1 | **Mangling Talons** | *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 22 (4d10) slashing damage, and the target must make a *Strength Saving Throw:* DC 13. *Failure:* The target suffers a rending wound. While wounded, the target has disadvantage on Strength, Dexterity, and Constitution d20 Tests, and its speed is halved. The wound ends if the creature regains 15 or more hit points at once, or if the target or a creature within 5 feet of it uses an action to stanch the wound by succeeding on a Wisdom (Medicine) check: DC 15.|
| 2 | **Bone Spike** | *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 16 (3d10) piercing damage. If the spawn moved at least 20 feet straight toward the target immediately before this hit and the target is Large or smaller, it is impaled on the spike and becomes grappled (escape DC 15). While grappled, the target is restrained and takes 5 (1d10) piercing damage at the start of each of the Chaos Spawn’s turns. |
| 3 | **War Stomp** | *Dexterity or Strength Saving Throw (target’s choice):* DC 15, each other creature in a 10-foot emanation from the spawn. If the ground in that area is loose earth or stone, it becomes difficult terrain until cleared. *Failure:* A creature takes 11 (2d10) bludgeoning damage and is knocked prone. |
| 4 | **Flesh Feast** | *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 16 (3d10) piercing damage, and the spawn regains hit points equal to the damage dealt. |
| 5 | **Blood Disgorge** | *Constitution Saving Throw:* DC 15, each creature in a 30-foot cone. *Failure:* 16 (3d10) necrotic damage and the creature can't regain hit points until the start of the spawn’s next turn. *Success:* Half damage only. |
| 6 | **Murderous Fit** | The spawn’s speed increases by 20 feet until the end of its turn, and it may make up to three attacks. Each attack must be against a different target. *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 16 (3d10) bludgeoning damage. |

##### Spawn of Change Table
| 1d6 | Actions | Effect |
|:---:|:-----------|:-----------|
| 1 | **Transmuting Grasp** | *Melee Spell Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 15 ft., *Hit:* 22 (4d10) force damage, and the target must make a *Charisma saving throw:* DC 15. *Failure:* It suffers a mutation* (mutation save DC 15). |
| 2 | **Warping Breath** | *Charisma Saving Throw:* DC 15, each creature in a 30-foot cone. *Failure:* A creature takes 11 (2d10) force damage and is teleported to an unoccupied space of the spawn's choice that it can see within the cone's area. The chosen space must be on a surface or in a liquid that can support the target without needing to squeeze. *Success:* Half damage only. |
| 3 | **Molten Liquids** | *Ranged or Melee Spell Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft. or range 30/120 ft., *Hit:* 27 (5d10) fire damage. |
| 4 | **Burning Limbs** | *Melee Spell Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 15 ft., *Hit:* 16 (3d10) fire damage. If the target is a creature or a flammable object, it ignites. Until a creature takes an action to douse the fire, the target takes 11 (2d10) fire damage at the end of each of its turns. |
| 5 | **Unstable Field** | The spawn gains 20 temporary hit points until the start of its next turn. If a creature damages the spawn with an attack while within 30 feet of it and the spawn still has these temporary hit points, the attacker takes 5 (1d10) lightning damage. |
| 6 | **Disruptive Slam** | *Melee Spell Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 22 (4d10) bludgeoning damage, and the target is sheathed in chaotic energy until the start of the spawn’s next turn. If the target casts a spell before then, it takes 22 (4d10) force damage and the effect ends. |

| 2 | **Acidic Bile** | *Dexterity Saving Throw:* DC 15, each creature in a 30-foot cone. *Failure:* A creature is covered in acid until it or another creature uses an action to scrape or wash the acid off. While covered in acid, the creature takes 16 (3d10) acid damage at the end of each of its turns. |

If the target is a creature, it must attempt a *Constitution Saving Throw:* DC 15. *Failure:* The target becomes withered, causing it to only deal half damage with its attacks. It repeats the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success. |
| 4 | **Nauseating Visage** | *Wisdom Saving Throw:* DC 15, each other creature in a 30-foot emanation from the spawn. *Failure:* The creature is frightened of the spawn and repeats the save at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success. |
| 5 | **Sticky Mucus** | *Ranged Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, range 30/120 ft., *Hit:* 16 (3d10) bludgeoning damage, and the target is restrained by sticky mucus until it is destroyed (AC 15; 20 HP; immune to bludgeoning, necrotic, poison, and psychic damage). |
| 6 | **Gift of Infestation** | *Melee Weapon Attack:* +7 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 11 (2d10) piercing damage, and insects burrow into the target’s flesh, infesting it. While infested, the target takes 11 (2d10) piercing damage at the end of each of its turns. Any creature within reach can use an action to make a DC 15 Wisdom (Medicine) check to remove the insects using a weapon or object that deals fire, piercing, or slashing damage, causing 1d10 damage of the same type to the target. On a success, the effect ends. A creature can choose to make the check more aggressively, gaining advantage, but if it does, the target instead takes 2d10 damage. |

| 1 | **Toxic Fangs** | *Melee Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, reach 10 ft., *Hit:* 38 (7d10) piercing damage, and the target must make a *Constitution saving throw:* DC 15. *Failure:* The target is poisoned and repeats the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success. |
| 2 | **Acidic Bile** | *Dexterity Saving Throw:* DC 18, each creature in a 60-foot cone. *Failure:* A creature is covered in acid until it or another creature uses an action to scrape or wash the acid off. While covered in acid, the creature takes 27 (5d10) acid damage at the end of each of its turns. |
| 3 | **Withering Touch** | *Melee Spell Attack:* +10 to hit, reach 5 ft., *Hit:* 27 (5d10) necrotic damage. If the target is a creature, it must attempt a *Constitution Saving Throw:* DC 18. *Failure:* The target becomes withered, causing it to only deal half damage with its attacks. It repeats the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success. |
| 4 | **Nauseating Visage** | *Wisdom Saving Throw:* DC 18, each other creature in a 60-foot emanation from the spawn. *Failure:* A creature is frightened of the spawn and repeats the saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effect on a success. |
| 5 | **Sticky Mucus** | *Ranged Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, range 60/150 ft., *Hit:* The target takes 27 (5d10) bludgeoning damage and is restrained by sticky mucus until it is destroyed (AC 17; 30 HP; immune to bludgeoning, necrotic, poison, and psychic damage). |
| 6 | **Gift of Infestation** | *Melee Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, reach 10 ft., *Hit:* The target takes 22 (4d10) piercing damage, and insects burrow into its flesh, infesting it. While infested, the target takes 22 (4d10) piercing damage at the end of each of its turns. Any creature within reach can use an action to attempt a DC 18 Wisdom (Medicine) check to remove the insects using a weapon or object that deals fire, piercing, or slashing damage, causing 1d10 damage of the same type to the target on a success, ending the effect. A creature can choose to make the check more aggressively, gaining advantage, but if it does, the target instead takes 4d10 damage. |

### Spawn of Chaos Loot
Valuable spawn of chaos loot typically comes from harvested materials and usually requires a **Wisdom (Survival)** or **Intelligence (Arcana)** check. You may also allow players proficient in specific tools to harvest relevant items (e.g., a **Wisdom (Leatherworker’s Tools)** check to gather Hide). 

Alternatively, you can roll for loot randomly using a flat modifier.

##### Lesser Spawn of Chaos Loot (Avg. 27gp)

| Looting Check Result <br> or 1d20 + 3 |  Loot  |
|:---:|:-----------:|
|  1-5  | 1d4(2) 5gp Item (10gp) |
|  6-8 | 1d6(3) 5gp Items (15gp) | 
|  9-16 | 1d4(2) 10gp Items (20gp) |  
|  17-21 | 1d4(2) 20gp Items (40gp)  |  
|  22+ |  1d6(3) 20gp Items (60gp) |

|  8-10 | 2d8(9) 5gp Items (45gp) | 
|  11-18 | 1d12(6) 10gp Items (60gp) |  
|  19-22 | 1d12(6) 20gp Items (60gp)  |

#### Optional: Describing Looted Materials
If you’re not interested in the specifics, simply say the party collected materials worth the rolled gp value. If you want more detail, the tables below suggest materials for different gp values by creature. They also provide **Example Names** and **Quality Descriptors** for items worth **half** or **twice** the table's gp value.

For example, a 10gp Bone item from a spawn could be a Twisted Claw, a 5gp version might be a Cracked Twisted Claw, and a 20gp version could be a Superior Twisted Claw.

***When To Use Descriptions.*** You can describe these items during looting, when selling them, or when crafting, but it's best not to make players track long descriptive names. Only use as much detail as is needed when needed.

#### Optional: Magic Loot for Item Crafting
If you plan to use these creatures’ loot for crafting magic items, consult the Magic Themes table for thematic suggestions. The **Magic Theme** column helps align the crafted item’s effects with the creature’s nature, while the **Example Descriptor** suggests how to describe the loot's magical quality. Magic loot can span one or multiple themes.
 
For example, Chaotic loot could be used to craft items that warp space or time or produce unpredictable effects.
 
***Random Magic Ingredients.***
To introduce randomness to how often magic loot is found, roll a percentile die along with the normal loot roll to see if magic loot is found. There's a suggested probability at the top of the table.

##### Spawn of Chaos Magic Themes 
**Suggested Chance of Finding Magic Loot: 80%**
|1d4 | Magic Theme | Example Descriptor | 
|:--:|:---:|:-----------:|
| 1-2 <br>  | Chaotic (Eldritch/Realty-Warping)| Chaos-Infused| 
| 3-4   | Fiendish  | Demonic|  

***Magic Loot GP Values.*** The value of magic ingredients depends on your crafting system. Subtract their cost from the normal loot’s gp value. If the ingredient is worth significantly more, subtract it from the next treasure hoard instead.

## Stoneheart

Stoneheart was once a powerful warlord <br> commanding a formidable beastman tribe, known <br> for his brutal strength and unwavering dominance. His reign was challenged when a cunning bray speaker attempted to seize control of the tribe by possessing Stoneheart’s body, intending to use the mighty minotaur as a puppet to command the tribe. However, Stoneheart’s will proved to be extraordinarily powerful. In a remarkable feat of mental fortitude, he managed to wrest control of his body long enough to exact vengeance on the shaman’s physical form, which lay vulnerable and defenseless in a trance.

After Stoneheart destroyed the shaman's body, the shaman’s spirit became trapped within him. This left the two entities locked in a constant battle for control. When Stoneheart is in control, he behaves and fights like a typical minotaur doombull, exuding raw power and engaging in relentless, brutal combat. However, when the shaman’s spirit gains the upper hand, Stoneheart’s capabilities change dramatically. Under the shaman’s influence, he gains access to mystic powers, allowing him to wield dark magic and curses far beyond the reach of ordinary minotaurs.



\columnbreak


<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>

This duality makes Stoneheart a fearsome and unpredictable foe. The shaman’s spirit grants him a level of cunning and strategic thinking that is unheard of among minotaurs, making him a dangerous opponent on and off the battlefield. However, the constant internal struggle between the two spirits also renders him prone to erratic and unpredictable behavior. Allies and enemies alike are never certain which aspect of Stoneheart they will face: the unyielding brute force of the doombull or the dark, cunning sorcery of the trapped shaman. This internal conflict drives Stoneheart’s actions, making him one of the most formidable and enigmatic figures among the beastmen.


 <img src='https://i.ibb.co/g45MTVF/Rage-Scarred-Berserker-Theros-Beyond-Death-Art-1024x752.jpg' style='position:absolute;right:-170px;top:-15px;width:1080px;transform:scaleX(1)' />

___
___
> ## Stoneheart
> *Large monstrosity (beastman), chaotic evil*
> ___
> - **Armor Class** 16 (natural armor)
> - **Hit Points** 315 (30d10+150)
> - **Speed** 40 ft.
>___
>|STR|DEX|CON|INT|WIS|CHA|
>|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|:---:|
>|22 (+6)|11 (+0)|20 (+5)|6 (-2)|20 (+5)|14 (+2)|
>___
> - **Saving Throws** Str +11, Iin +3, Cha +7
> - **Skills** Athletics +12, Perception +17, Intimidation +14, Stealth +6, Survival +12
> - **Senses** darkvision 60 ft., passive Perception 26
> - **Languages** Abyssal
> - **Challenge** 17 (18,000 XP) &emsp;&emsp; **Proficiency Bonus** +6
> ___
>
> ***Blood Greed.*** At the end of each turn, if Stoneheart dealt damage to a creature this turn, it goes berserk until the end of its next turn. While berserk, it deals an extra 9 (2d8) damage on hit with weapon attacks.
>
> ***Brute.*** A melee weapon deals one extra die of its damage when Stoneheart hits with it (included in the attack).
>
> ***Corrupting Influence.*** At the start of Stoneheart's turn, each creature under the effects of his spells or cursed by his Atrophy Bolt takes 10 (3d6) necrotic damage.
>
> ***Labyrinthine Recall.*** Stoneheart can perfectly recall any path he has traveled.
>
> ***Land's Stride.*** Moving through nonmagical difficult terrain does not cost Stoneheart extra movement.
>
> ***Possessed.*** At the end of each turn, if Stoneheart took 30 or more damage and was not already Possessed, he makes a DC 18 Charisma saving throw. On a failure, he is Possessed by the spirit, changing his Intelligence to 10 (Int +6), ending any Berserk effects, and making his concentration unbreakable. If Stoneheart takes 30 or more damage in a turn while Possessed, he can attempt another Charisma saving throw to end the Possession and any spells he has cast.
>
> ### Actions
>
> ***Multiattack.*** Stoneheart makes two attacks.
>
> ***Dazing Gore.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +12 to hit, reach 5 ft., one creature. *Hit:* 18 (3d8 + 6) piercing damage. If Stoneheart moved at least 20 feet straight toward the target immediately before the hit, the target takes an extra 13 (3d8) piercing damage. If the target is a creature, it must succeed on a DC 19 Strength saving throw or be pushed up to 10 feet away and knocked prone. If the target fails by 10 or more, the creature is dazed until the end of its next turn.
>
> ***Hewing Greataxe.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +12 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 25 (3d12 + 6) slashing damage. The target must succeed on a DC 18 Strength saving throw, or Stoneheart automatically hits the target with another Hewing Greataxe attack as part of this action. If the target fails by 10 or more, the attack is a critical hit.
>
> ***Tackle.*** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +12 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target. *Hit:* 4 (1d8) bludgeoning damage. If Stoneheart moved at least 20 feet straight toward the target immediately before the hit, the target takes an extra 13 (3d8) bludgeoning damage.
>
> ***Wing Puncturing Javelin.*** *Melee or Ranged Weapon Attack:* +12 to hit, reach 5 ft. or range 30/120 ft., one target. *Hit:* 16 (3d6 + 6) damage in melee or 12 (2d6 + 6) piercing damage at range. If the attack targets a flying creature, it has advantage, and on hit, the target must succeed on a DC 19 Strength saving throw or be knocked prone and dazed until the end of the creature until the end of its next turn.
>
> ***Atrophy Bolt (Only While Possessed).*** *Ranged Spell Attack:* +11 to hit, range 150 ft., one target. *Hit:* 10 (3d6) necrotic damage, and the target is cursed for 1 minute or until Stoneheart is no longer possessed.
>
> ***Spellcasting (Only While Possessed).*** Stoneheart is a spellcaster. His spellcasting ability is Wisdom (spell save DC 18, +10 to hit with spell attacks). He knows the following spells:
> - **3/Day:** *devolve** (5th level), *impending doom** (5th level), *vile tide** (5th level)
>
> **New Spells Found Later in Document*
>
> ### Bonus Action
>
> ***Battle Cast.*** When Stoneheart uses his action to cast a spell, he can make one weapon attack or two Atrophy Bolt attacks.
>
> ### Legendary Actions
> Stoneheart can take 3 legendary actions, choosing from the options below. Only one legendary action option can be used at a time and only at the end of another creature's turn. Stoneheart regains spent legendary actions at the start of its turn.
>
> **Check.** Stoneheart makes a skill check that would normally require an action.
>
> **Dark Surge (Only While Possessed).** Stoneheart moves up to 20 feet in a straight line then makes an Atrophy Bolt attack.
>
> **Move.** Stoneheart moves up to 20 feet without provoking attacks of opportunity.
>
> **Slam.** Stoneheart moves up to 20 feet in a straight line then makes a Tackle attack.
>
> **Tenacious Will.** If Stoneheart is suffering from an effect that allows him to make a saving throw at the beginning or end of his turn, he may immediately make that save against the effect with advantage. He can use this legendary action while incapacitated.
>



\pagebreakNum


### Epic Battle: Dual Souls

For an epic encounter with Stoneheart, give the Bray Speaker spirit possessing him its own pool of 310 hit points, which it regains after a short or long rest. 

Whenever Stoneheart takes damage while possessed, the damage is instead dealt to the Bray Speaker. If this damage reduces the Bray Speaker to 0 hit points, Stoneheart takes the remaining damage and loses the Possessed trait. Conversely, if Stoneheart is reduced to 0 hit points, the Bray Speaker takes the remaining damage. In this case, the Stoneheart automatically becomes possessed, losing the ability to make saving throws to end the possession.

Stoneheart only dies if both he and the Bray Speaker are reduced to 0 hit points.

For this encounter, increase Stoneheart's challenge rating (CR) to 22.

### Stoneheart Tactics

#### Not Possessed
* Engages primarily in melee combat.
* **Typical Attack Sequence:** 
    * Gores a target, follows with a strike from his Hewing Greataxe.
    * If movement permits, may gore two different targets.
    * Against aerial opponents, uses Wing Puncturing Javelin.
* Utilizes legendary actions to maximize movement and damage output.



#### Possessed

* Shifts to a spellcasting role, focusing on area control and debuffs.
* Maintains distance from opponents
* Starts turns by maximizing Corrupting Influence effects, targeting multiple opponents with spells.
* **Sequence in combat:**
    * Casts a spell
    * Follows up with Hewing Greataxe for close <Br> targets, or Atrophy Blot for ranged attacks.
    * Uses legendary actions  for Dark Surge to <br> maintain battlefield control.

<br>

* Mogis's Favor - Uriah Voth, <br> Wizards of the Coast
* Bloodforged Battle-Axe - <Br> Alayna Danner, <br> Wizards of the Coast

\columnbreak

##### Spells
&emsp;**Devolve:** Casts on creatures concentrating on spells of 5th level or higher.

**Vile Tide:** Used when it can target two or more opponents.

**Impending Doom:** Default choice when other spells aren't optimal.



##### Stoneheart Adventures

 | d4  | Plot Hook |
|:---:|:-----------:|
|  1  | **The Dual Threat:** The players are tasked with stopping a series of brutal raids on nearby settlements. As they investigate, they discover that the raids are led by Stoneheart, who is unpredictably alternating between savage attacks and cunning ambushes.|
|  2  |**The Blood Moon:** A rare celestial event known as the Blood Moon is approaching, during which Stoneheart plans to perform a dark ritual to permanently merge with the shaman’s spirit, becoming an even greater threat.|
|  3  | **The Siege of Darkwood:** Stoneheart’s tribe has laid siege to a fortified town, using both brute force and dark magic to breach the defenses. The players must infiltrate the besieging forces, disrupt the shaman’s influence, and find a way to break the siege |
|  4  | **A New Puppet:** The players discover that the shaman’s spirit is attempting to transfer itself into a new, equally powerful host while keeping Stoneheart as a puppet. They must stop this transfer, battling the shaman's chosen vessel and ensuring that both Stoneheart and the shaman’s spirit are defeated.  |

### Stoneheart Loot
Most of the valuable goods that can be looted from minotaurs are the remains of the equipment they were using or valuables they were carrying, though it is common to harvest horns from their fallen. Most dropped valuables can be found using an **Intelligence (Investigation)** check.

Alternatively, you can roll for the loot randomly using a flat modifier.

#### Stoneheart Loot Tables
The following tables describe the number of items and value of those items the players are able to loot depending on the result of their check or the results of your roll. If they're making checks, you can have them make a separate check for each creature they're looting or use one check for multiple creatures at once to save time.

## New Conditions
The following are new status conditions referenced by various spells, magic items, and creature abilities throughout the document.

#### Berserk
Berserk creatures gain the following effects unless an ability states otherwise:
* The creature can only use its movement to move closer to an enemy it can see or hear.
* The creature can only use its action, bonus action, and reaction to make melee attacks or move closer to an enemy it can see or hear.
* The creature can't maintain concentration on spells or other effects.
* The creature can't be frightened or charmed.

#### Dazed 
A dazed creature can’t take reactions and on its turn, it must choose whether it gets a move, an action, or a bonus action; it gets only one of the three.

#### Emboldened 
The creature is momentarily filled with boisterous confidence, causing it to deal an additional 7 (2d6) damage when it hits with an attack. This condition lasts up to 1 minute. The condition ends early if, at the end of the creature's turn, it missed with all its attacks that turn, it is Charmed or Frightened, or it is under the effects of the *calm emotions* spell.

##### New Condition Art Credit
* Spatial Contortion - Daarken, Wizards of the Coast

\columnbreak

#### Mutated
When a creature is affected by this condition, it suffers one of the random mutations described in the Mutation Table below. A creature can't suffer from two instances of the same mutation at once.

Unless an ability states otherwise, a creature suffering from one or more mutations can make a Charisma saving throw at the end of each of its turns, ending the effects of all mutations on a success. The save DC is equal to the highest save DC among any effects that inflicted it with its current mutations.

##### Mutation Table
| d6  | Mutation |  Creature Effect  |
|:---:|:---------:| :---------:|
|  1  |  Wild Spasms | The creature can't take reactions, and on each of its turns it must choose whether it gets a move, an action, or a bonus action; it gets only one of the three. |
|  2  | Degeneration  | The creature's form becomes brittle.  While a creature is brittle, any attack that hits the creature is a critical hit.|
|  3  | Twisted Arms |  The creature can no longer wield weapons or cast spells with somatic components and it has disadvantage on all weapon attack rolls.|
|  4  | Inverted Eyes | The creature is blinded.|
|  5  | Gelatinous Legs | The creature falls prone and can't stand up.|
|  6  | Regeneration | The creature regains 10 hit points at the start of its turn if it has at least 1 hit point.|

#### Quickened
A quickened creature gains an additional action on each of its turns. That action can be used only to take the Attack (one weapon attack or unarmed strike only), Dash, Disengage, Hide, or Use an Object action. The *haste* spell applies the quickened condition among its other effects, and a creature cannot benefit from the quickened condition from multiple sources at once.

<img src='https://i.postimg.cc/XqTgjPw5/2892-spatial-contortion.jpg' style='position:absolute;left:-0px;bottom:-570px;width:816px;transform:scaleX(1)' />
